An introduction to
the ‘glatos’ R package:





Chris Holbrook, Tom Binder, Darryl Hondorp, Nancy Nate
Jon Pye, Ryan Gosse, Caitlin Bate (Ocean Tracking Network)

Annual GLATOS Coordination Meeting
Feb 27 2020, Ann Arbor, Michigan

Why an R package?


Raw Data

Access
Wrangle
Check, clean
Summarize
Explore
Analyze

Products

Why an R package?



  • Consistent (standardization)
  • Reproducible
  • Efficient
  • Accessible
  • Transparent



Community-driven best practices

Installing the package


OTN Gitlab

https://gitlab.oceantrack.org/GreatLakes/glatos

library(remotes)
install_url("https://gitlab.oceantrack.org/GreatLakes/glatos/repository/master/archive.zip",
              build_opts = c("--no-resave-data", "--no-manual"))
library(glatos)
## version 0.4.1 ('full-english-breakfast')


A set of tools for:


Data loading

  • Read project workbook data
  • Read detection data
  • Read receiver location data
  • Read tag specs
    • Convert ‘raw’ sensor measurements to ‘real’ (depth in meters)

A set of tools for:


Filtering and summarizing

  • False detection filter
  • Compress detections into discrete events
  • Simple summaries
    • by fish
    • by receiver/location
  • Residence time
  • Array evaluation

A set of tools for:


Exploration and visualization

  • Graphical movement histories
  • Distribution maps
    • presence-absence data
    • fine-scale positions
  • Animations
    • interpolating between detections
    • making and editing video files

A set of tools for:


Simulation

  • Code collisions
    • selecting tag specs
  • Virtual fish in virtual receiver networks
    • receiver line spacing
    • receiver array tradeoffs (grids vs lines)

Load Project Workbook data

wb <- read_glatos_workbook(wb_file = "HECSL_GLATOS_20170818.xlsm")

False detection filter

  • Uses min_lag ‘short interval’ criteria
    • see Pincock 2012 - Vemco technical note
##       transmitter_id receiver_sn detection_timestamp_utc min_lag passed_filter
## 61484          40148      109410     2016-06-11 02:09:28     295             1
## 61487          40148      109410     2016-06-11 02:14:23     295             1
## 61535          40148      109410     2016-06-11 03:35:13    4850             0
## 42515          40148      109431     2016-05-23 07:35:23     331             1
## 42531          40148      109431     2016-05-23 07:40:54     135             1
## 42543          40148      109431     2016-05-23 07:43:09      88             1
  • Single detections will not pass filter
##       transmitter_id receiver_sn detection_timestamp_utc min_lag passed_filter

## 39208          40148      119189     2016-05-22 05:35:29      NA             0
## 23337          40148      119332     2016-05-19 02:15:05     115             1

False detection filter

det <- false_detections(det, tf = 3600)
## The filter identified 1045 (0.97%) of 107727 detections as potentially false.

Distribution maps

Animating tracks

  • interpolate positions between detections (e.g., hourly, around land, etc.)
    • interpolate_path
  • make set of images (frames)
    • make_frames
  • stitch images to video
    • make_video
